<h2 id="anatomy" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Anatomy<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#anatomy"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>To set up the pagination correctly, you&#x27;ll need to understand its anatomy and
how we name its parts.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute to help identify them in the DOM.</p>
</blockquote>

<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the pagination package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> pagination</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/pagination&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>The pagination package exports two key functions:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - State machine logic.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
</ul>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Pass a unique <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">useMachine</code> so generated element ids stay predictable.</p>
</blockquote>

<h3 id="controlled-page" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlled page<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlled-page"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">page</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onPageChange</code> to control the current page externally.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>pagination<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">count</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">500</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>

</span><span class="code-line">  page<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onPageChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">setPage</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">page</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="controlled-page-size" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlled page size<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlled-page-size"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">pageSize</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onPageSizeChange</code> to control page size.</p>

</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">count</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">500</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  pageSize<span class="token punctuation">,</span>

</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="initial-page-and-page-size" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Initial page and page size<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#initial-page-and-page-size"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>

<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>pagination<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

<h3 id="link-based-pagination" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Link-based pagination<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#link-based-pagination"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">type: &quot;link&quot;</code> and provide <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getPageUrl</code> to render real navigation links.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>pagination<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword control-flow">return</span> <span class="token template-string"><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span><span class="token string">/products?page=</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">page</span><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">&amp;pageSize=</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">pageSize</span><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>

<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>pagination<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="customizing-accessibility-labels" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Customizing accessibility labels<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#customizing-accessibility-labels"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">translations</code> to customize trigger and page labels.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>pagination<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function-variable function">itemLabel</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter"><span class="token punctuation">{</span> page<span class="token punctuation">,</span> totalPages <span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token template-string"><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span><span class="token string">Page </span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${</span>page<span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string"> of </span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${</span>totalPages<span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span></span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the pagination&#x27;s items */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>

<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The pagination machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ root: string; ellipsis: (index: number) =&gt; string; firstTrigger: string; prevTrigger: string; nextTrigger: string; lastTrigger: string; item: (page: number) =&gt; string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the elements in the accordion. Useful for composition.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">translations</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">IntlTranslations</code><span class="d_block">Specifies the localized strings that identifies the accessibility elements and their states</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">count</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">Total number of data items</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">pageSize</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The controlled number of data items per page</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultPageSize</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The initial number of data items per page when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the page size of the pagination.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">siblingCount</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">Number of pages to show beside active page</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">boundaryCount</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">Number of pages to show at the beginning and end</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">page</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The controlled active page</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultPage</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The initial active page when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the active page of the pagination.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onPageChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: PageChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Called when the page number is changed</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onPageSizeChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: PageSizeChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Called when the page size is changed</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">type</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;button&quot; | &quot;link&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The type of the trigger element</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getPageUrl</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: PageUrlDetails) =&gt; string</code><span class="d_block">Function to generate href attributes for pagination links.
Only used when `type` is set to &quot;link&quot;.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dir</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;ltr&quot; | &quot;rtl&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The document&#x27;s text/writing direction.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The unique identifier of the machine.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getRootNode</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; ShadowRoot | Node | Document</code><span class="d_block">A root node to correctly resolve document in custom environments. E.x.: Iframes, Electron.</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The pagination <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">page</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The current page.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">count</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The total number of data items.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">pageSize</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The number of data items per page.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">totalPages</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The total number of pages.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">pages</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Pages</code><span class="d_block">The page range. Represented as an array of page numbers (including ellipsis)</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">previousPage</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The previous page.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">nextPage</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The next page.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">pageRange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">PageRange</code><span class="d_block">The page range. Represented as an object with `start` and `end` properties.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">slice</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&lt;V&gt;(data: V[]) =&gt; V[]</code><span class="d_block">Function to slice an array of data based on the current page.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">setPageSize</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(size: number) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to set the page size.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">setPage</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(page: number) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to set the current page.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">goToNextPage</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">VoidFunction</code><span class="d_block">Function to go to the next page.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">goToPrevPage</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">VoidFunction</code><span class="d_block">Function to go to the previous page.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">goToFirstPage</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">VoidFunction</code><span class="d_block">Function to go to the first page.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">goToLastPage</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">VoidFunction</code><span class="d_block">Function to go to the last page.</span></li></ul>

multiple pages.\n\n\u003cResources pkg=\"@zag-js/pagination\" /\u003e\n\n\u003cShowcase id=\"Pagination\" /\u003e\n\n## Installation\n\nInstall the pagination package:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"pagination/installation.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\nTo set up the pagination correctly, you'll need to understand its anatomy and\nhow we name its parts.\n\n\u003e Each part includes a `data-part` attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"pagination\" /\u003e\n\n## Usage\n\nImport the pagination package:\n\n```jsx\nimport * as pagination from \"@zag-js/pagination\"\n```\n\nThe pagination package exports two key functions:\n\n- `machine` - State machine logic.\n- `connect` - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\n\n\u003e Pass a unique `id` to `useMachine` so generated element ids stay predictable.\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"pagination/usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n```jsx\nconst api = pagination.connect(service)\n\n// You can slice the data, to get data for current page\nconst currentPageData = data.slice(api.pageRange.start, api.pageRange.end)\n\napi.page\n// =\u003e 1\n\napi.setPage(3)\n// page =\u003e 3\n\napi.previousPage\n// =\u003e 2\n\napi.nextPage\n// =\u003e 4\n\napi.pages\n/*\n    [\n      {\n        \"type\": \"page\",\n        \"value\": 1,\n      },\n      {\n        \"type\": \"page\",\n        \"value\": 2,\n      },\n      {\n        \"type\": \"ellipsis\",\n      },\n      {\n        \"type\": \"page\",\n        \"value\": 3,\n      },\n      {\n        \"type\": \"page\",\n        \"value\": 4,\n      },\n    ]\n*/\n\napi.pageRange\n// =\u003e { start: 4, end: 13 }\n```\n\n### Controlled page\n\nUse `page` and `onPageChange` to control the current page externally.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(pagination.machine, {\n  count: 500,\n  pageSize: 20,\n  page,\n  onPageChange(details) {\n    setPage(details.page)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Controlled page size\n\nUse `pageSize` and `onPageSizeChange` to control page size.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(pagination.machine, {\n  count: 500,\n  pageSize,\n  onPageSizeChange(details) {\n    setPageSize(details.pageSize)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Initial page and page size\n\nUse `defaultPage` and `defaultPageSize` for uncontrolled initial values.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(pagination.machine, {\n  count: 500,\n  defaultPage: 3,\n  defaultPageSize: 20,\n})\n```\n\n### Link-based pagination\n\nSet `type: \"link\"` and provide `getPageUrl` to render real navigation links.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(pagination.machine, {\n  count: 500,\n  type: \"link\",\n  getPageUrl(details) {\n    return `/products?page=${details.page}\u0026pageSize=${details.pageSize}`\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Customizing visible page ranges\n\nUse `siblingCount` and `boundaryCount` to control how many page items are shown.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(pagination.machine, {\n  count: 500,\n  siblingCount: 2,\n  boundaryCount: 2,\n})\n```\n\n### Customizing accessibility labels\n\nUse `translations` to customize trigger and page labels.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(pagination.machine, {\n  count: 500,\n  translations: {\n    rootLabel: \"Results pages\",\n    prevTriggerLabel: \"Previous page\",\n    nextTriggerLabel: \"Next page\",\n    itemLabel: ({ page, totalPages }) =\u003e `Page ${page} of ${totalPages}`,\n  },\n})\n```\n\n## Styling guide\n\nEach part includes a `data-part` attribute you can target in CSS.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"root\"] {\n  /* styles for the pagination's root */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"item\"] {\n  /* styles for the pagination's items */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"ellipsis\"] {\n  /* styles for the pagination's ellipsis */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"prev-trigger\"] {\n  /* styles for the pagination's previous page trigger */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"next-trigger\"] {\n  /* styles for the pagination's next page trigger */\n}\n\n/* We add a data-disabled attribute to the prev/next items when on the first/last page  */\n\n[data-part=\"prev-trigger\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for the pagination's previous page trigger when on first page */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"next-trigger\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for the pagination's next page trigger when on first page */\n}\n```\n\n## Methods and Properties\n\n### Machine Context\n\nThe pagination machine exposes the following context properties:\n\n\u003cContextTable name=\"pagination\" /\u003e\n\n### Machine API\n\nThe pagination `api` exposes the following methods:\n\n\u003cApiTable name=\"pagination\" /\u003e\n\n### Data Attributes\n\n\u003cDataAttrTable name=\"pagination\" /\u003e"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"5:[\"$\",\"$Le\",null,{\"doc\":{\"title\":\"Pagination\",\"description\":\"Using the pagination
